  <script type="text/javascript">
   function getTagToken() {
            if(window.location.search === '') {
                return 'home';
            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('/a/browse/') !== -1) {
                return 'category';
            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('/catalog/search.do') !== -1) {
                return 'search';
            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('/a/products/') !== -1) {
                return 'product';
            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('/cart/') !== -1) {
                return 'cart';
            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('/cm/') !== -1) {
                return 'coremedia';
            } else if (window.location.href.indexOf('/checkout/') !== -1) {
                return 'checkout';
            } else {
                return 'other';
            }
        }

        function getReleaseBuildStamp() {
            var buildStamp = '';
            for(var i=0;i<document.childNodes.length;i++){
                if(document.childNodes[i].nodeType === 8){
                    buildStamp = document.childNodes[i].data.split('EDT - REV - ')[1];
                    break;
                }
            }
            return buildStamp || '';
        }

        window.newrelic && newrelic.addRelease('unknown', getReleaseBuildStamp().trim() || 'not-defined');
        window.newrelic && newrelic.setPageViewName(getTagToken() || 'other');
        window.newrelic && newrelic.setCustomAttribute('cloneId', window.cloneID);
  </script>

				function noAtobDecode(str) {
					var keyStr = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/=";
					var retval = "", chr1, chr2, chr3 = "", enc1, enc2, enc3, enc4 = "", i = 0;
			
					// remove all characters that are not A-Z, a-z, 0-9, +, /, or =
					var base64test = /[^A-Za-z0-9\+\/\=]/g;
					if (base64test.exec(str)) {
						retval = false;
					} else {
						str = str.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9\+\/\=]/g, "");
						do {
							enc1 = keyStr.indexOf(str.charAt(i++));
							enc2 = keyStr.indexOf(str.charAt(i++));
							enc3 = keyStr.indexOf(str.charAt(i++));
							enc4 = keyStr.indexOf(str.charAt(i++));
							chr1 = (enc1 << 2) | (enc2 >> 4);
							chr2 = ((enc2 & 15) << 4) | (enc3 >> 2);
							chr3 = ((enc3 & 3) << 6) | enc4;

								retval = retval + String.fromCharCode(chr2);

						retval = unescape(retval);
					}
					return retval;
				}

					}
